032|
033|4. **LiveCareer**  
034|   - **Pros:** Provides a comprehensive suite of job search tools, including resume and cover letter builders.  
035|   - **Cons:** Some templates may not be ATS-friendly, pricing can be confusing.
036|
037|5. **Resumake**  
038|   - **Pros:** Free to use, simple and straightforward interface, no sign-up required.  
039|   - **Cons:** Limited features compared to paid services, fewer templates available.

001|# Resume Writing Service PRD

003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language:** English
005|- **Project Name:** resume_writing_service

008|## 2. Product Definition
009|### Product Goals:
010|1. Create a polished, ATS-friendly resume tailored for Network/RF Engineers.
011|2. Highlight achievements and skills in Python automation effectively.
012|3. Provide deliverables in both Word and PDF formats, along with an optional LinkedIn summary.
013|
014|### User Stories:
015|1. As a Network/RF Engineer, I want a resume that showcases my skills in Python automation so that I can attract potential employers.
016|2. As a job seeker, I want my resume to be ATS-friendly to ensure it passes through automated screening systems.
017|3. As a professional, I want my resume to be available in both Word and PDF formats for easy submission.
018|
019|### Competitive Analysis:
020|
021|1. **TopResume**  
022|   - **Pros:** Offers free resume reviews, extensive resources for job seekers, and a user-friendly interface.  
023|   - **Cons:** Higher pricing compared to some competitors, limited customization options.
024|
025|2. **ResumeGenius**  
026|   - **Pros:** Provides templates specifically designed for ATS compatibility, easy-to-use resume builder.  
027|   - **Cons:** Limited personal touch in writing, may not cater specifically to engineers.
028|
029|3. **Zety**  
030|   - **Pros:** Offers a wide range of templates and customization options, includes cover letter builder.  
031|   - **Cons:** Subscription model can be costly, some users report issues with customer service.
032|
033|4. **LiveCareer**  
034|   - **Pros:** Provides a comprehensive suite of job search tools, including resume and cover letter builders.  
035|   - **Cons:** Some templates may not be ATS-friendly, pricing can be confusing.
036|
037|5. **Resumake**  
038|   - **Pros:** Free to use, simple and straightforward interface, no sign-up required.  
039|   - **Cons:** Limited features compared to paid services, fewer templates available.
040|### Competitive Analysis:
041|To be filled in later.
042|
043|### Requirements Analysis:

046|2. **User-Friendly Interface:** The service should provide an intuitive interface for users to input their information easily.
047|3. **Multiple Formats:** The ability to generate resumes in both Word and PDF formats is essential.
048|4. **Customization Options:** Users should have the ability to customize their resumes to highlight specific skills and achievements.
049|5. **LinkedIn Summary:** An optional feature to create a LinkedIn summary based on the resume content.

018|
